      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses in the 11th century
       </b>
       . During the period 1001 to 1100 there were 241
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 84 were partial, 90 were annular, 61 were total, and 6 were hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year was four, occurring in 11 different years: 1009, 1027, 1045, 1052, 1060, 1063, 1074, 1081, 1092, 1096, and 1099. One month, May 1063, had two eclipses.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Dates are given using the
       <a href="/wiki/Julian_calendar" title="Julian calendar">
        Julian calendar
       </a>
       .
      </p>
